Hemihedral twinning is a special case of merohedral twinning. It only involves two distinct domains. Pseudo-merohedral twinning is a subclass merohedral twinning in which lattice is coincidentally superimposable. In the case of non-merohedral or epitaxial twinning the reciprocal lattices do not superimpose exactly. A37, 517-525; erratum (1981), A37, 921.
